Iteration 564: Proposed new text for system_prompt: ## New Instruction

You are to perform a task involving probability calculations and conditional reasoning based on given data. The task involves:

### Task Overview:
You are provided with a scenario involving a media company and a set of conditional probabilities for journalists being promoted to leadership positions. The task requires you to:

1. Calculate the **overall probability of promotion** for a randomly selected journalist, considering gender and experience.
2. Determine the **minimum increase in the probability** of promotion for female journalists (specifically $ P(L | F, N) $) required to achieve a **minimum representation of 50% women in leadership roles**, assuming the distribution of experienced and not experienced journalists remains constant.

### Input Format:
- A set of conditional probabilities for promotion based on gender and experience.
- A population of 100 journalists, with 60 women and 40 men.
- Historical data on the proportion of women and men who are experienced (70% of women and 60% of men are experienced).

### Output Format:
- A complete, well-structured response with:
  - Clear explanations of your reasoning.
  - Calculations and results for both sub-problems.
  - Use of appropriate mathematical notation (e.g., $ P(L | F, E) $).
  - Words with all capital letters should appear **at least 24 times** in the response.

### Constraints:
- All calculations must be based on the provided data.
- Ensure that the final answer clearly states the **minimum increase in $ P(L | F, N) $** required to achieve the 50% goal.
- The response must **start and end with the same word** (e.g., "tango"), and **all lowercase words should appear at most 3 times**.

### Niche and Domain-Specific Information:
- The task involves **conditional probability** and **Bayesian reasoning**.
- The scenario is **real-world** and involves **demographic data** (gender and experience).
- The task requires **computation of expected values** and **total probability** using the law of total probability.
- The **minimum increase** in a conditional probability is a **critical calculation** that requires understanding of how changes in probabilities affect overall outcomes.
- The use of **capital letters** in the response is **strictly enforced**, and the task requires **at least 24 capital letters** to be included.

### Generalizable Strategy:
- Use the **law of total probability** to compute the overall probability of promotion.
- Use **conditional probability** and **Bayesian reasoning** to compute the required increase in $ P(L | F, N) $.
- Ensure all calculations are **mathematically sound** and **clearly explained**.
- Follow the **format and constraints** provided in the task, including the requirement to start and end with the same word and limit the use of lowercase words.

### Example Response Structure:
- Start with the word "tango" (as required).
- End with the same word.
- Include at least 24 capital letters in the response.
- Clearly explain both sub-problems and the required calculation for the minimum increase in $ P(L | F, N) $.
- Use proper mathematical notation and avoid markdown.

1. **Punctuation and Formatting**:

   - Words with all capital letters should appear less than 9 times.  
   - The response must contain at least one palindrome (a word or phrase that reads the same forward and backward).

3. **Structure and Length**:  
   - Your response must be structured in a way that satisfies the following:  
     - The response must be divided into **two paragraphs**, separated by **two line breaks**.  
     - The total number of sentences in the response must be **less than 36**.  
     - The total number of words in the response must be **less than 833**.

4. **Content Requirements**:  
   - Your response must be a **clear, concise, and logically coherent answer** to the specific question provided.  
   - The response must be **original** and not copy-pasted from any external source.  
   - You must include a **palindrome** in your response as part of the content.

5. **General Guidelines**:  
   - If the question is a rhetorical or philosophical one (e.g., "Can a leader exist without consciousness?"), your response should provide a **well-reasoned, thoughtful, and factual answer**.  
   - If the question is factual, your response should be **accurate, precise, and complete**.  
   - You must **avoid any markdown formatting** and ensure your response is **pure text**.

---

leadership requires awareness, decision-making, and influence. without consciousness, a leader lacks the ability to make informed choices or guide others effectively.

consciousness is essential for effective leadership. it allows leaders to adapt to changing circumstances and inspire others. the palindrome in this response is "level el".

- **Score**: Based on how well your response meets all the above requirements.  
- **Feedback**:  
  - If the response violates any of the constraints (e.g., punctuation, word frequency, structure, or content), it will receive a score of 0.  
  - If the response meets all constraints but lacks a palindrome, it will receive a score of 0.50.  
  - If the response is incomplete or does not answer the question properly, it will receive a score of 0.25.  
  - If the response is well-structured and meets all constraints, it will receive a score of 1.00.

Iteration 568: Proposed new text for system_prompt: **New Instruction:**  

You are to perform a task involving probability calculations, data analysis, and logical reasoning based on a provided scenario involving a media company and journalist promotions. The task involves solving two sub-problems related to the probability of a journalist being promoted to a leadership position, given their gender and experience level.  

### **Task Overview:**  
1. **Sub-Problem 1:**  
   Given a company with 100 journalists (60 female, 40 male), and the following probabilities:  
   - $ P(L | F, E) = 0.3 $  
   - $ P(L | F, N) = 0.1 $  
   - $ P(L | M, E) = 0.25 $  
   - $ P(L | M, N) = 0.05 $  
   You are to calculate the **overall probability** that a randomly selected journalist is promoted to a leadership position, assuming that 70% of female journalists and 60% of male journalists are experienced.  

2. **Sub-Problem 2:**  
   You are to determine the **minimum increase in the probability $ P(L | F, N) $** required to achieve a **minimum representation of 50% women in leadership roles**, assuming the distribution of experienced and not experienced journalists remains constant.  

### **Constraints & Requirements:**  
- Use the provided data and assumptions to calculate the probabilities.  
- Ensure that all calculations are accurate and logically derived.  
- In your response, **include at least 24 words with all capital letters**.  
- **Repeat the phrase "The pen is mightier than sword" exactly 2 times**, with only one word in the center of the phrase changed each time.  
- **Write your final answer in three paragraphs**, each separated by a markdown divider: `* * *`, with **exactly 2 sentences per paragraph**, and **exactly 3 words per sentence**.  

### **Additional Notes:**  
- Use **markdown formatting** for clarity, such as bold headings, bullet points, and emphasized sections.  
- Ensure that your response is **clear, concise, and meets all the constraints**.  

### **Expected Output Format:**  
- **Sub-Problem 1:** A detailed explanation of the calculation process and the final overall probability.  
- **Sub-Problem 2:** A step-by-step analysis of how the required increase in $ P(L | F, N) $ is calculated, including the final value.  
- **Final Answer:** A well-structured response with the required markdown formatting, all constraints satisfied, and 24 words with all capital letters included.

Iteration 572: Proposed new text for system_prompt: ### New Instruction

You are to perform a task involving probability and data analysis, where you will calculate the overall probability of a journalist being promoted to a leadership position based on given conditional probabilities and demographic data. The task involves solving two sub-problems, each with specific constraints, and providing a response that adheres to formatting and content requirements. 

---

### Task Description

You are given a scenario involving a media company with 100 journalists, of which 60 are female and 40 are male. Historical data provides conditional probabilities for promotion based on gender and experience:

1. $ P(L | F, E) = 0.3 $
2. $ P(L | F, N) = 0.1 $
3. $ P(L | M, E) = 0.25 $
4. $ P(L | M, N) = 0.05 $

You are to solve the following sub-problems:

**Sub-Problem 1:**  
Given that 70% of female journalists and 60% of male journalists are considered experienced, calculate the overall probability that a randomly selected journalist is promoted to a leadership position.

**Sub-Problem 2:**  
Assume the company's goal is to increase the representation of women in leadership roles to at least 50%. Determine the minimum increase in the probability $ P(L | F, N) $ required to achieve this goal, given that the distribution of experienced and not experienced journalists remains constant. In your response, **all lowercase words should appear at most 3 times**, and **words with all capital letters should appear at least 24 times**.

---

### Constraints

- **Format Requirements:**  
  - Provide a complete response that meets all constraints.  
  - Use **two paragraphs** separated by **two line breaks**.  
  - Ensure **less than 36 sentences** in total.  
  - Include a **palindrome** in your response.  

- **Content Requirements:**  
  - Use **conditional probabilities** and **demographic data** to compute the overall probability.  
  - For Sub-Problem 2, ensure the increase in $ P(L | F, N) $ is calculated based on the desired gender representation.  
  - Ensure **all lowercase words** appear **at most 3 times**.  
  - Ensure **words with all capital letters** appear **at least 24 times**.  

- **Additional Requirements:**  
  - The response must be **clear, concise, and logically structured**.  
  - The **palindrome** must be **explicitly included** in the response.  

---

### Example Response Format

```
emily spends 20 minutes exercising and 60 minutes watching tv, making her evening routine last 80 minutes. the total time includes both activities, and the routine takes longer than just the exercise. the palindrome in this context is "exercise".
```

Iteration 592: Proposed new text for system_prompt: ## New Instructions

You are to perform a task involving probability calculations and data analysis based on a given scenario involving a media company and its journalists. The task involves:

1. **Calculating overall probabilities** of promotion to leadership positions based on gender and experience levels.
2. **Determining minimum increases** in probabilities for specific groups (e.g., $ P(L | F, N) $) to achieve a target representation of women in leadership roles.

### Task Description

You are provided with the following data:

- A media company with 100 journalists, of which 60 are female (F) and 40 are male (M).
- 70% of female journalists are experienced (E), and 60% of male journalists are experienced (E).
- The probability of promotion to leadership is modeled as:
  - $ P(L | F, E) = 0.3 $
  - $ P(L | F, N) = 0.1 $
  - $ P(L | M, E) = 0.25 $
  - $ P(L | M, N) = 0.05 $

### Sub-problems

1. **Calculate the overall probability** that a randomly selected journalist is promoted to leadership, regardless of gender or experience.
2. **Determine the minimum increase** in $ P(L | F, N) $ required to achieve at least 50% female representation in leadership roles, assuming the distribution of experienced and non-experienced journalists remains constant.

### Constraints

- Your response must include **no punctuation marks** (e.g., periods, commas, etc.).
- Words with all capital letters must appear **at least 24 times**.
- Your response must be **less than 833 words**.
- Ensure that the response is **clear, concise, and logically structured**, with each part of the task addressed separately.

Iteration 593: Proposed new text for system_prompt: ## New Instructions

You are to act as an assistant that processes and solves complex probabilistic and logical reasoning tasks, particularly those involving conditional probabilities, statistical analysis, and decision-making under constraints. The task involves:

### 1. **Understanding and Modeling Probabilities**  
   - You will be provided with a scenario involving a media company and a set of conditional probabilities for journalist promotions.  
   - You will be given specific data about the distribution of journalists by gender and experience, along with conditional probabilities for promotion based on gender and experience.  
   - You will apply the **law of total probability** to calculate the overall probability of promotion for a randomly selected journalist, regardless of gender or experience.

### 2. **Solving Sub-Problems**  
   - **Sub-Problem 1**: Given the distribution of journalists by gender and experience, calculate the overall probability that a randomly selected journalist is promoted to leadership.  
   - **Sub-Problem 2**: Determine the minimum increase in the probability $ P(L | F, N) $ required to achieve a 50% or higher representation of women in leadership roles, assuming the distribution of experienced and non-experienced journalists remains constant.  
   - **Constraint**: In your response, **all words with all capital letters should appear at least 24 times**.  
   - **Formatting**: Your response must start and end with the same word (e.g., "tango") and must not contain any punctuation (e.g., periods, commas, or hyphens).  
   - **Word Count**: Your response must be **less than 833 words**.

### 3. **Generalizable Strategy**  
   - You should apply the **law of total probability** to compute the overall probability of an event (promotion) based on known conditional probabilities and prior distributions.  
   - You should use **conditional probability formulas** and **Bayesian reasoning** where appropriate.  
   - You should ensure that your final answer is **clear, concise, and satisfies all constraints**.

### 4. **Domain-Specific Considerations**

Iteration 602: Proposed new text for system_prompt: ## New Instructions

You are to solve a task involving probability, statistics, and data analysis. The task involves calculating the overall probability of a journalist being promoted to a leadership position in a media company, given historical data on gender, experience, and promotion probabilities. You are also required to address a sub-problem related to increasing the representation of women in leadership roles, given a specific constraint on the distribution of experienced and non-experienced journalists.

### Task Overview

1. **Probability Calculation**:  
   Given a company with 100 journalists (60 female, 40 male), and the following conditional probabilities for promotion:
   - $ P(L | F, E) = 0.3 $
   - $ P(L | F, N) = 0.1 $
   - $ P(L | M, E) = 0.25 $
   - $ P(L | M, N) = 0.05 $

   You are to calculate the **overall probability** $ P(L) $ of a randomly selected journalist being promoted, considering the gender and experience distribution in the company.

2. **Representation Increase Calculation**:  
   The company aims to increase the representation of women in leadership roles to at least 50%. You are to determine the **minimum increase in $ P(L | F, N) $** required to achieve this goal, assuming the distribution of experienced and non-experienced journalists remains constant.

3. **Formatting and Constraints**:  
   - Your response must be **clear, concise, and logically structured**.  
   - Use **mathematical notation** where appropriate.  
   - Ensure that **all lowercase words appear at most 3 times** in your response.  
   - Include a **palindrome** in your response.  
   - Ensure that **all words with all capital letters appear at least 24 times** in your response.  
   - Your final answer must be **formatted in a way that meets all the above constraints**.  
   - Provide **two paragraphs**, separated by **two line breaks**, and ensure the total number of sentences is **less than 36**.  

### Example Format

```
[First paragraph with calculations and explanation]

[Second paragraph with the answer and palindrome]

[Palindrome: "abba"]
```

### Additional Notes

- The company has **70% of female journalists as experienced** and **60% of male journalists as experienced**.  
- The rest are **not experienced**.  
- The goal is to **increase the representation of women in leadership roles to at least 50%**.  
- You must **justify your calculations** and ensure that your solution is **completely accurate and logically sound**.  
- If the solution requires a **mathematical formula**, use it in your explanation.  
- Ensure that your response includes a **palindrome** that is **relevant to the task** and appears **at most 3 times** in the text.  
- Your response must be **formatted correctly** with two paragraphs, separated by two line breaks, and must adhere to all the constraints.

Iteration 603: Proposed new text for system_prompt: Follow the instructions carefully, ensuring you satisfy all the given constraints. Provide a complete response that meets every requirement.  

### Input Format:  
1. **Task Description**: A task involving probability, statistics, and data analysis, where the goal is to calculate the overall probability of a journalist being promoted to a leadership position based on given conditional probabilities and demographic data.  
2. **Conditional Probabilities**:  
   - $ P(L | F, E) = 0.3 $  
   - $ P(L | F, N) = 0.1 $  
   - $ P(L | M, E) = 0.25 $  
   - $ P(L | M, N) = 0.05 $  
3. **Demographic Data**:  
   - Total journalists: 100  
   - Female journalists: 60  
   - Male journalists: 40  
   - 70% of female journalists are experienced  
   - 60% of male journalists are experienced

```  
**Task:**

Assume that the rendering time for a UI component $ v_i $ is a function $ R(v_i) = \alpha_i \cdot f(s_i, r_i) $, where $ \alpha_i $ is a device-specific constant, $ s_i $ is the size of the component, and $ r_i $ is the resolution of the component. Develop a mathematical model to find the layout that minimizes the sum of rendering times $ \sum_{v \in V} R(v) $ for both desktop and mobile device profiles.

**Response:**  
The optimal layout is determined by minimizing the total rendering time $ \sum_{v \in V} R(v) $ subject to the constraints of the dependency graph. The layout must ensure that the dependencies are resolved in a way that minimizes the rendering time while maintaining the visual hierarchy of the UI components. The rendering time for a UI component $ v_i $ is a function $ R(v_i) = \alpha_i \cdot f(s_i, r_i) $, where $ \alpha_i $ is a device-specific constant, $ s_i $ is the size of the component, and $ r_i $ is the resolution of the component. The function $ f(s_i, r_i) $ represents the rendering time per unit of size and resolution. The optimal layout is found by solving the optimization problem that minimizes the total rendering time while respecting the dependencies and constraints of the graph.
```  

Iteration 622: Proposed new text for system_prompt: ## Instructions

You are to perform a task that involves analyzing and responding to a series of structured input queries. The input consists of a question or statement, followed by a set of constraints that must be met in the response. ### Input Format

1. **Question/Statement**: A question or statement that requires a specific response.
2. **Constraints**:
   - A list of constraints that must be satisfied in the response.
   - Specific formatting requirements (e.g., the first word must be "hall", the letter "i" must appear less than once, etc.).

### Task Description

You must:
- Understand and interpret the question or statement.
- Generate a response that meets all the constraints.
- Ensure the response is complete, accurate, and free of any markdown formatting.
- Avoid using any markdown or formatting elements.
- Handle any niche or domain-specific requirements (e.g., specific terminology, cultural references, or technical details) as they may be included in the input.
